<s> we immediately lett her down but severall raw hands jumping in her and unfortunately the plug being out she almost filled with water which caused such confusion that the canoe gott on board before we gott from our side <\s>
<s> our hands went on board to demand him but they gott all their arms and wou'd not suffer us to board them <\s>
<s> when they returned wou'd not suffer them to return with their arms to take them out for fear of some accident <\s>
<s> of the little privateer came on board of us to know the reason of the disturbance between his people and ours <\s>
<s> told him the reason and forbid him to carry that fellow away for if he did he might chance to hear of him in the west indies and if he did hee'd go 100 leagues to meet him and hee'd take ten for one and murroone 23 his voyage and send him home to his owners and give his people a good dressing i dont doubt but he'll be as good as his word opened a bb <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning with a great deal of rain <\s>
<s> footnote 23 maroon _saturday 4th this morning about 5 am <\s>
<s> came in a ship from marble head 24 who was bound to so <\s>
<s> she had lost her main mast mizen mast and fore top mast <\s>
<s> in the latitude 35Â ° she mett with a hard gale of wind which caused this dissaster so was obliged to put back and came to new york to refitt <\s>
<s> about 11 clock the _humming bird weighd anchor for philadelphia to gett hands <\s>
<s> with 2 sergeants belonging to capt <\s>
<s> riggs comp 25 came on board to look for some soldiers that was suspected to be on board the _humming bird but the wind and tide proving contrary was obliged to return she laying att coney island <\s>
<s> att 6 came in a ship from lisbon had 7 weeks passage and a sloop from turks island both loaded with salt <\s>
<s> the ship appearing to be a lofty vessell put our people in a panetick fear taking her for a 70 gun ship and as we had severall deserters from the men a war they desired the capt <\s>
<s> to hoist a v reef in the jack and lower our penant for a signal for our pinnace that was then a shoare that if she proved to be a man of war they might gett ashoar and gett clear from the press 26 but it proved quit the contrary for the ship and sloops crew taking us by the signal that we had made for our pinnace for a tender of a man of war that was laying there to press hands they quited their vessells and run a shoare as soon as they saw our pinnace mann'd and made for the bushes <\s>
<s> att night the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch to recover them of their fright <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning all this day <\s>
<s> footnote 24 marblehead mass footnote 25 richard riggs brother-in-law of john watts was captain of one of the two independent companies of fusiliers stationed at new york footnote 26 press-gang _sunday 5th att 5 am <\s>
<s> shipt a hand mathias sallam <\s>
<s> our mate went a shoar to fill water <\s>
<s> he came on board about 8 and informed us that the two country sloops lay att the hook and only waited for a pilott to bring them up which hope will prove true being all tyred of staying here <\s>
<s> weighd anchor and gott nearer in shoar to gett out of the current <\s>
<s> rainy squally windy weather <\s>
<s> here lyes a brigt <\s>
<s> bound to newfoundland a ship to jamaica and a sloop which att 6 pm <\s>
<s> weigh'd anchor bound to barbadoes loaded with lumber and horses <\s>
<s> of beef and 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> this day being a month since we left our commission port have sett down what quantity of provisions expended with the provisions att broch 27 viz <\s>
<s> of beef 1 bb <\s>
<s> of pork 14 bb <\s>
<s> remains 49-1 2 bb <\s>
<s> of beef 29 bb <\s>
<s> of pork 40 c <\s>
<s> footnote 27 at broach means that had been opened _munday 6th about 6 am <\s>
<s> came in the two country sloops so long waited for <\s>
<s> they had been fitted out to cruise after a spanish privateer that was cruising on the coast and had taken severall of our english vessells also a ship from newfoundland and the _huming bird privateer who had been to meet them to gett some hands <\s>
<s> langoe comm'r of one of the above sloops when he came a longside of us he gave us three chears and we returned him the same <\s>
<s> went up to york to gett a doctor and some hands <\s>
<s> one promist him to give an answer the next day <\s>
<s> att 10 a hand came on board to list but went away without signing <\s>
<s> he promist to return again his name was john webb <\s>
<s> _tuesday 7th this morning the capt <\s>
<s> went up to york and at last agreed with a doctor that belong'd to capt <\s>
<s> cunningham 28 com'r of one of the privateer's sloop that came in the day before <\s>
<s> his name is william blake a young gentleman well recomended by the gen'n of york <\s>
<s> returned on board and brought with him a chest of medicines a doctor's box which cost Â £ 20 york cur renc y 29 also 10 pistolls and cutlasses <\s>
<s> footnote 28 george cunningham whose commission was ordered may 8 1741 footnote 29 the currencies of the different colonies were in great confusion on account of the various and extensive issues of paper money which was greatly depreciated in value <\s>
<s> apparently a pound in new york currency was in 1741 worth about 2.25 mexican silver dollars a pound in rhode island currency about 85 of a dollar <\s>

<s> footnote 30 after careening a vessel and scrubbing off the ooze and shells etc it was customary to coat the bottom with a mixture of tallow sulphur etc <\s>
<s> this was called giving her boot-tops _friday 10th att 9 am <\s>
<s> the mas'r went in the pinnace to york to fetch the lieut <\s>
<s> came in 2 sloops edwd <\s>
<s> seymore and john pasco in comp'y with a brigt james walker com'r all from antigua 13 days passage but brings no news <\s>
<s> came on board the mas'r with 4 new hands john webb jerem'h henderson william ramsey and jos <\s>
<s> the negro servant to the lieut <\s>
<s> _saturday 11 about 8 am <\s>
<s> vandam 31 came on board to take his leave of the capt <\s>
<s> he brought with him 2 pistolls and an acct <\s>
<s> of the doctors chest and other things found for him which amounts to Â £ 38.2 1 new york currency 32 which is carry to acct <\s>
<s> att 10 the lieut <\s>
<s> and doctor came on board in the pilott boat with the hands that had left us since we were at york only 3 which viz <\s>
<s> webster price and ferrows <\s>
<s> the tide being spent cou'd not sail but resolv'd to sail the next day <\s>
<s> went a shoar to gett some hands that had promist to come on board when we were ready to sail <\s>
<s> vandam went from the side we gave him three guns and three chears <\s>
<s> gave the people a bowl of punch <\s>

<s> with severall hands that went ashoar the night before came on board with our pilott <\s>
<s> the tide being almost spent coud not sail <\s>
<s> duncan mckenley a fitt person for that post <\s>
<s> he wetted his commission by giving the people a tub of punch <\s>
<s> opened 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _munday 13th weigh'd from stratton island with 61 hands officers included <\s>
<s> anchord about 2 pm <\s>
<s> freebody by the capt <\s>
<s> sent him a list of our hands and an acct <\s>
<s> of our provisions and charges together with the lieut <\s>
<s> name to gett it registred in the admiralty office att rhode island <\s>
<s> quartered the people to the guns viz <\s>
<s> went up to york with seven hands three of which left viz <\s>
<s> northwood colson and taylor <\s>
<s> a sloop came in from newfoundland brings no news also another sloop from bermudas <\s>
<s> _friday 3d att 5 am <\s>
<s> we perceived the three hands that had left us the day before on board the _humming bird privateer who had been inticed by some of the owners to leave us by making of them drunk <\s>
<s> about 10 we saw their canoe going a shoare with our hands in her also joseph ferrow whom we had brought from rhode island and had since rec'd clothes on board but had entered on board that sloop as boatswain <\s>

<s> henderson above means harriman footnote 32 see the account below and notes 29 and 33 _sunday 12th the lieut <\s>
<s> with severall hands that went ashoar the night before came on board with our pilott <\s>
<s> the tide being almost spent coud not sail <\s>
<s> duncan mckenley a fitt person for that post <\s>
<s> he wetted his commission by giving the people a tub of punch <\s>
<s> opened 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _munday 13th weigh'd from stratton island with 61 hands officers included <\s>
<s> anchord about 2 pm <\s>
<s> freebody by the capt <\s>
<s> sent him a list of our hands and an acct <\s>
<s> of our provisions and charges together with the lieut <\s>
<s> name to gett it registred in the admiralty office att rhode island <\s>
<s> quartered the people to the guns viz <\s>
<s> went up to york with seven hands three of which left viz <\s>
<s> northwood colson and taylor <\s>
<s> a sloop came in from newfoundland brings no news also another sloop from bermudas <\s>
<s> _friday 3d att 5 am <\s>
<s> we perceived the three hands that had left us the day before on board the _humming bird privateer who had been inticed by some of the owners to leave us by making of them drunk <\s>
<s> about 10 we saw their canoe going a shoare with our hands in her also joseph ferrow whom we had brought from rhode island and had since rec'd clothes on board but had entered on board that sloop as boatswain <\s>
<s> as soon as they had done watering and returning aboard we mann'd our pinnace and boarded their canoe and took our three hands out of her also joseph ferrow and brought them aboard <\s>
<s> some time after the _humming bird's canoe coming alonside ferrow jumpt in her and they put off our pinnace being hawld up in the tackles <\s>
<s> we immediately lett her down but severall raw hands jumping in her and unfortunately the plug being out she almost filled with water which caused such confusion that the canoe gott on board before we gott from our side <\s>
<s> our hands went on board to demand him but they gott all their arms and wou'd not suffer us to board them <\s>
<s> when they returned wou'd not suffer them to return with their arms to take them out for fear of some accident <\s>
<s> of the little privateer came on board of us to know the reason of the disturbance between his people and ours <\s>
<s> told him the reason and forbid him to carry that fellow away for if he did he might chance to hear of him in the west indies and if he did hee'd go 100 leagues to meet him and hee'd take ten for one and murroone 23 his voyage and send him home to his owners and give his people a good dressing i dont doubt but he'll be as good as his word opened a bb <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning with a great deal of rain <\s>
<s> footnote 23 maroon _saturday 4th this morning about 5 am <\s>
<s> came in a ship from marble head 24 who was bound to so <\s>
<s> she had lost her main mast mizen mast and fore top mast <\s>
<s> in the latitude 35Â ° she mett with a hard gale of wind which caused this dissaster so was obliged to put back and came to new york to refitt <\s>
<s> about 11 clock the _humming bird weighd anchor for philadelphia to gett hands <\s>
<s> with 2 sergeants belonging to capt <\s>
<s> riggs comp 25 came on board to look for some soldiers that was suspected to be on board the _humming bird but the wind and tide proving contrary was obliged to return she laying att coney island <\s>
<s> att 6 came in a ship from lisbon had 7 weeks passage and a sloop from turks island both loaded with salt <\s>
<s> the ship appearing to be a lofty vessell put our people in a panetick fear taking her for a 70 gun ship and as we had severall deserters from the men a war they desired the capt <\s>
<s> to hoist a v reef in the jack and lower our penant for a signal for our pinnace that was then a shoare that if she proved to be a man of war they might gett ashoar and gett clear from the press 26 but it proved quit the contrary for the ship and sloops crew taking us by the signal that we had made for our pinnace for a tender of a man of war that was laying there to press hands they quited their vessells and run a shoare as soon as they saw our pinnace mann'd and made for the bushes <\s>
<s> att night the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch to recover them of their fright <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning all this day <\s>
<s> footnote 24 marblehead mass footnote 25 richard riggs brother-in-law of john watts was captain of one of the two independent companies of fusiliers stationed at new york footnote 26 press-gang _sunday 5th att 5 am <\s>
<s> shipt a hand mathias sallam <\s>
<s> our mate went a shoar to fill water <\s>
<s> he came on board about 8 and informed us that the two country sloops lay att the hook and only waited for a pilott to bring them up which hope will prove true being all tyred of staying here <\s>
<s> weighd anchor and gott nearer in shoar to gett out of the current <\s>
<s> rainy squally windy weather <\s>
<s> here lyes a brigt <\s>
<s> bound to newfoundland a ship to jamaica and a sloop which att 6 pm <\s>
<s> weigh'd anchor bound to barbadoes loaded with lumber and horses <\s>
<s> of beef and 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> this day being a month since we left our commission port have sett down what quantity of provisions expended with the provisions att broch 27 viz <\s>
<s> of beef 1 bb <\s>
<s> of pork 14 bb <\s>
<s> remains 49-1 2 bb <\s>
<s> of beef 29 bb <\s>
<s> of pork 40 c <\s>
<s> footnote 27 at broach means that had been opened _munday 6th about 6 am <\s>
<s> came in the two country sloops so long waited for <\s>
<s> they had been fitted out to cruise after a spanish privateer that was cruising on the coast and had taken severall of our english vessells also a ship from newfoundland and the _huming bird privateer who had been to meet them to gett some hands <\s>
<s> langoe comm'r of one of the above sloops when he came a longside of us he gave us three chears and we returned him the same <\s>
<s> went up to york to gett a doctor and some hands <\s>
<s> one promist him to give an answer the next day <\s>
<s> att 10 a hand came on board to list but went away without signing <\s>
<s> he promist to return again his name was john webb <\s>
<s> _tuesday 7th this morning the capt <\s>
<s> went up to york and at last agreed with a doctor that belong'd to capt <\s>
<s> cunningham 28 com'r of one of the privateer's sloop that came in the day before <\s>
<s> his name is william blake a young gentleman well recomended by the gen'n of york <\s>
<s> returned on board and brought with him a chest of medicines a doctor's box which cost Â £ 20 york cur renc y 29 also 10 pistolls and cutlasses <\s>
<s> footnote 28 george cunningham whose commission was ordered may 8 1741 footnote 29 the currencies of the different colonies were in great confusion on account of the various and extensive issues of paper money which was greatly depreciated in value <\s>
<s> apparently a pound in new york currency was in 1741 worth about 2.25 mexican silver dollars a pound in rhode island currency about 85 of a dollar <\s>

<s> the negro servant to the lieut <\s>

<s> gave the people a pale of punch <\s>
<s> footnote 30 after careening a vessel and scrubbing off the ooze and shells etc it was customary to coat the bottom with a mixture of tallow sulphur etc <\s>
<s> this was called giving her boot-tops _friday 10th att 9 am <\s>
<s> the mas'r went in the pinnace to york to fetch the lieut <\s>
<s> came in 2 sloops edwd <\s>
<s> seymore and john pasco in comp'y with a brigt james walker com'r all from antigua 13 days passage but brings no news <\s>
<s> came on board the mas'r with 4 new hands john webb jerem'h henderson william ramsey and jos <\s>
<s> the negro servant to the lieut <\s>
<s> _saturday 11 about 8 am <\s>
<s> vandam 31 came on board to take his leave of the capt <\s>
<s> he brought with him 2 pistolls and an acct <\s>
<s> of the doctors chest and other things found for him which amounts to Â £ 38.2 1 new york currency 32 which is carry to acct <\s>
<s> att 10 the lieut <\s>
<s> and doctor came on board in the pilott boat with the hands that had left us since we were at york only 3 which viz <\s>
<s> webster price and ferrows <\s>
<s> the tide being spent cou'd not sail but resolv'd to sail the next day <\s>
<s> went a shoar to gett some hands that had promist to come on board when we were ready to sail <\s>
<s> vandam went from the side we gave him three guns and three chears <\s>
<s> gave the people a bowl of punch <\s>
<s> footnote 31 this was probably isaac van dam merchant son of president rip van dam <\s>
<s> henderson above means harriman footnote 32 see the account below and notes 29 and 33 _sunday 12th the lieut <\s>
<s> with severall hands that went ashoar the night before came on board with our pilott <\s>
<s> the tide being almost spent coud not sail <\s>
<s> duncan mckenley a fitt person for that post <\s>
<s> he wetted his commission by giving the people a tub of punch <\s>
<s> opened 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _munday 13th weigh'd from stratton island with 61 hands officers included <\s>
<s> anchord about 2 pm <\s>
<s> freebody by the capt <\s>
<s> sent him a list of our hands and an acct <\s>
<s> of our provisions and charges together with the lieut <\s>
<s> name to gett it registred in the admiralty office att rhode island <\s>
<s> quartered the people to the guns viz <\s>
<s> went up to york with seven hands three of which left viz <\s>
<s> northwood colson and taylor <\s>
<s> a sloop came in from newfoundland brings no news also another sloop from bermudas <\s>
<s> _friday 3d att 5 am <\s>
<s> we perceived the three hands that had left us the day before on board the _humming bird privateer who had been inticed by some of the owners to leave us by making of them drunk <\s>
<s> about 10 we saw their canoe going a shoare with our hands in her also joseph ferrow whom we had brought from rhode island and had since rec'd clothes on board but had entered on board that sloop as boatswain <\s>
<s> as soon as they had done watering and returning aboard we mann'd our pinnace and boarded their canoe and took our three hands out of her also joseph ferrow and brought them aboard <\s>
<s> some time after the _humming bird's canoe coming alonside ferrow jumpt in her and they put off our pinnace being hawld up in the tackles <\s>
<s> we immediately lett her down but severall raw hands jumping in her and unfortunately the plug being out she almost filled with water which caused such confusion that the canoe gott on board before we gott from our side <\s>
<s> our hands went on board to demand him but they gott all their arms and wou'd not suffer us to board them <\s>
<s> when they returned wou'd not suffer them to return with their arms to take them out for fear of some accident <\s>
<s> of the little privateer came on board of us to know the reason of the disturbance between his people and ours <\s>
<s> told him the reason and forbid him to carry that fellow away for if he did he might chance to hear of him in the west indies and if he did hee'd go 100 leagues to meet him and hee'd take ten for one and murroone 23 his voyage and send him home to his owners and give his people a good dressing i dont doubt but he'll be as good as his word opened a bb <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning with a great deal of rain <\s>
<s> footnote 23 maroon _saturday 4th this morning about 5 am <\s>
<s> came in a ship from marble head 24 who was bound to so <\s>
<s> she had lost her main mast mizen mast and fore top mast <\s>
<s> in the latitude 35Â ° she mett with a hard gale of wind which caused this dissaster so was obliged to put back and came to new york to refitt <\s>
<s> about 11 clock the _humming bird weighd anchor for philadelphia to gett hands <\s>
<s> with 2 sergeants belonging to capt <\s>
<s> riggs comp 25 came on board to look for some soldiers that was suspected to be on board the _humming bird but the wind and tide proving contrary was obliged to return she laying att coney island <\s>
<s> att 6 came in a ship from lisbon had 7 weeks passage and a sloop from turks island both loaded with salt <\s>
<s> the ship appearing to be a lofty vessell put our people in a panetick fear taking her for a 70 gun ship and as we had severall deserters from the men a war they desired the capt <\s>
<s> to hoist a v reef in the jack and lower our penant for a signal for our pinnace that was then a shoare that if she proved to be a man of war they might gett ashoar and gett clear from the press 26 but it proved quit the contrary for the ship and sloops crew taking us by the signal that we had made for our pinnace for a tender of a man of war that was laying there to press hands they quited their vessells and run a shoare as soon as they saw our pinnace mann'd and made for the bushes <\s>
<s> att night the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch to recover them of their fright <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning all this day <\s>
<s> footnote 24 marblehead mass footnote 25 richard riggs brother-in-law of john watts was captain of one of the two independent companies of fusiliers stationed at new york footnote 26 press-gang _sunday 5th att 5 am <\s>
<s> shipt a hand mathias sallam <\s>
<s> our mate went a shoar to fill water <\s>
<s> he came on board about 8 and informed us that the two country sloops lay att the hook and only waited for a pilott to bring them up which hope will prove true being all tyred of staying here <\s>
<s> weighd anchor and gott nearer in shoar to gett out of the current <\s>
<s> rainy squally windy weather <\s>
<s> here lyes a brigt <\s>
<s> bound to newfoundland a ship to jamaica and a sloop which att 6 pm <\s>
<s> weigh'd anchor bound to barbadoes loaded with lumber and horses <\s>
<s> of beef and 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> this day being a month since we left our commission port have sett down what quantity of provisions expended with the provisions att broch 27 viz <\s>
<s> of beef 1 bb <\s>
<s> of pork 14 bb <\s>
<s> remains 49-1 2 bb <\s>
<s> of beef 29 bb <\s>
<s> of pork 40 c <\s>
<s> footnote 27 at broach means that had been opened _munday 6th about 6 am <\s>
<s> came in the two country sloops so long waited for <\s>
<s> they had been fitted out to cruise after a spanish privateer that was cruising on the coast and had taken severall of our english vessells also a ship from newfoundland and the _huming bird privateer who had been to meet them to gett some hands <\s>
<s> langoe comm'r of one of the above sloops when he came a longside of us he gave us three chears and we returned him the same <\s>
<s> went up to york to gett a doctor and some hands <\s>
<s> one promist him to give an answer the next day <\s>
<s> att 10 a hand came on board to list but went away without signing <\s>
<s> he promist to return again his name was john webb <\s>
<s> _tuesday 7th this morning the capt <\s>
<s> went up to york and at last agreed with a doctor that belong'd to capt <\s>
<s> cunningham 28 com'r of one of the privateer's sloop that came in the day before <\s>
<s> his name is william blake a young gentleman well recomended by the gen'n of york <\s>
<s> returned on board and brought with him a chest of medicines a doctor's box which cost Â £ 20 york cur renc y 29 also 10 pistolls and cutlasses <\s>

<s> one promist him to give an answer the next day <\s>
<s> att 10 a hand came on board to list but went away without signing <\s>
<s> he promist to return again his name was john webb <\s>
<s> _tuesday 7th this morning the capt <\s>
<s> went up to york and at last agreed with a doctor that belong'd to capt <\s>
<s> cunningham 28 com'r of one of the privateer's sloop that came in the day before <\s>
<s> his name is william blake a young gentleman well recomended by the gen'n of york <\s>
<s> returned on board and brought with him a chest of medicines a doctor's box which cost Â £ 20 york cur renc y 29 also 10 pistolls and cutlasses <\s>
<s> footnote 28 george cunningham whose commission was ordered may 8 1741 footnote 29 the currencies of the different colonies were in great confusion on account of the various and extensive issues of paper money which was greatly depreciated in value <\s>
<s> apparently a pound in new york currency was in 1741 worth about 2.25 mexican silver dollars a pound in rhode island currency about 85 of a dollar <\s>

<s> gave the people a pale of punch <\s>
<s> of beef and a bb <\s>
<s> _thursday 9th this morning put our vessell on the carreen scrub her and gave her boot tops 30 att 4 pm <\s>
<s> our pilott came on board <\s>
<s> orderd him to attend on saturday morning for then he intended to sail <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch <\s>
<s> footnote 30 after careening a vessel and scrubbing off the ooze and shells etc it was customary to coat the bottom with a mixture of tallow sulphur etc <\s>
<s> this was called giving her boot-tops _friday 10th att 9 am <\s>
<s> the mas'r went in the pinnace to york to fetch the lieut <\s>
<s> came in 2 sloops edwd <\s>
<s> seymore and john pasco in comp'y with a brigt james walker com'r all from antigua 13 days passage but brings no news <\s>
<s> came on board the mas'r with 4 new hands john webb jerem'h henderson william ramsey and jos <\s>
<s> the negro servant to the lieut <\s>
<s> _saturday 11 about 8 am <\s>
<s> vandam 31 came on board to take his leave of the capt <\s>
<s> he brought with him 2 pistolls and an acct <\s>
<s> of the doctors chest and other things found for him which amounts to Â £ 38.2 1 new york currency 32 which is carry to acct <\s>
<s> att 10 the lieut <\s>
<s> and doctor came on board in the pilott boat with the hands that had left us since we were at york only 3 which viz <\s>
<s> webster price and ferrows <\s>
<s> the tide being spent cou'd not sail but resolv'd to sail the next day <\s>
<s> went a shoar to gett some hands that had promist to come on board when we were ready to sail <\s>
<s> vandam went from the side we gave him three guns and three chears <\s>
<s> gave the people a bowl of punch <\s>
<s> footnote 31 this was probably isaac van dam merchant son of president rip van dam <\s>
<s> henderson above means harriman footnote 32 see the account below and notes 29 and 33 _sunday 12th the lieut <\s>
<s> with severall hands that went ashoar the night before came on board with our pilott <\s>
<s> the tide being almost spent coud not sail <\s>
<s> duncan mckenley a fitt person for that post <\s>
<s> he wetted his commission by giving the people a tub of punch <\s>
<s> opened 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _munday 13th weigh'd from stratton island with 61 hands officers included <\s>
<s> anchord about 2 pm <\s>
<s> freebody by the capt <\s>
<s> sent him a list of our hands and an acct <\s>
<s> of our provisions and charges together with the lieut <\s>
<s> name to gett it registred in the admiralty office att rhode island <\s>
<s> quartered the people to the guns viz <\s>
<s> went up to york with seven hands three of which left viz <\s>
<s> northwood colson and taylor <\s>
<s> a sloop came in from newfoundland brings no news also another sloop from bermudas <\s>
<s> _friday 3d att 5 am <\s>
<s> we perceived the three hands that had left us the day before on board the _humming bird privateer who had been inticed by some of the owners to leave us by making of them drunk <\s>
<s> about 10 we saw their canoe going a shoare with our hands in her also joseph ferrow whom we had brought from rhode island and had since rec'd clothes on board but had entered on board that sloop as boatswain <\s>
<s> as soon as they had done watering and returning aboard we mann'd our pinnace and boarded their canoe and took our three hands out of her also joseph ferrow and brought them aboard <\s>
<s> some time after the _humming bird's canoe coming alonside ferrow jumpt in her and they put off our pinnace being hawld up in the tackles <\s>
<s> we immediately lett her down but severall raw hands jumping in her and unfortunately the plug being out she almost filled with water which caused such confusion that the canoe gott on board before we gott from our side <\s>
<s> our hands went on board to demand him but they gott all their arms and wou'd not suffer us to board them <\s>
<s> when they returned wou'd not suffer them to return with their arms to take them out for fear of some accident <\s>
<s> of the little privateer came on board of us to know the reason of the disturbance between his people and ours <\s>
<s> told him the reason and forbid him to carry that fellow away for if he did he might chance to hear of him in the west indies and if he did hee'd go 100 leagues to meet him and hee'd take ten for one and murroone 23 his voyage and send him home to his owners and give his people a good dressing i dont doubt but he'll be as good as his word opened a bb <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning with a great deal of rain <\s>
<s> footnote 23 maroon _saturday 4th this morning about 5 am <\s>
<s> came in a ship from marble head 24 who was bound to so <\s>
<s> she had lost her main mast mizen mast and fore top mast <\s>
<s> in the latitude 35Â ° she mett with a hard gale of wind which caused this dissaster so was obliged to put back and came to new york to refitt <\s>
<s> about 11 clock the _humming bird weighd anchor for philadelphia to gett hands <\s>
<s> with 2 sergeants belonging to capt <\s>
<s> riggs comp 25 came on board to look for some soldiers that was suspected to be on board the _humming bird but the wind and tide proving contrary was obliged to return she laying att coney island <\s>
<s> att 6 came in a ship from lisbon had 7 weeks passage and a sloop from turks island both loaded with salt <\s>
<s> the ship appearing to be a lofty vessell put our people in a panetick fear taking her for a 70 gun ship and as we had severall deserters from the men a war they desired the capt <\s>
<s> to hoist a v reef in the jack and lower our penant for a signal for our pinnace that was then a shoare that if she proved to be a man of war they might gett ashoar and gett clear from the press 26 but it proved quit the contrary for the ship and sloops crew taking us by the signal that we had made for our pinnace for a tender of a man of war that was laying there to press hands they quited their vessells and run a shoare as soon as they saw our pinnace mann'd and made for the bushes <\s>
<s> att night the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch to recover them of their fright <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning all this day <\s>
<s> footnote 24 marblehead mass footnote 25 richard riggs brother-in-law of john watts was captain of one of the two independent companies of fusiliers stationed at new york footnote 26 press-gang _sunday 5th att 5 am <\s>

<s> our mate went a shoar to fill water <\s>
<s> he came on board about 8 and informed us that the two country sloops lay att the hook and only waited for a pilott to bring them up which hope will prove true being all tyred of staying here <\s>
<s> weighd anchor and gott nearer in shoar to gett out of the current <\s>
<s> rainy squally windy weather <\s>
<s> here lyes a brigt <\s>
<s> bound to newfoundland a ship to jamaica and a sloop which att 6 pm <\s>
<s> weigh'd anchor bound to barbadoes loaded with lumber and horses <\s>

<s> our mate went a shoar to fill water <\s>
<s> he came on board about 8 and informed us that the two country sloops lay att the hook and only waited for a pilott to bring them up which hope will prove true being all tyred of staying here <\s>
<s> weighd anchor and gott nearer in shoar to gett out of the current <\s>
<s> rainy squally windy weather <\s>
<s> here lyes a brigt <\s>
<s> bound to newfoundland a ship to jamaica and a sloop which att 6 pm <\s>
<s> weigh'd anchor bound to barbadoes loaded with lumber and horses <\s>
<s> of beef and 1 tierce of bread <\s>

<s> footnote 27 at broach means that had been opened _munday 6th about 6 am <\s>
<s> came in the two country sloops so long waited for <\s>
<s> they had been fitted out to cruise after a spanish privateer that was cruising on the coast and had taken severall of our english vessells also a ship from newfoundland and the _huming bird privateer who had been to meet them to gett some hands <\s>
<s> langoe comm'r of one of the above sloops when he came a longside of us he gave us three chears and we returned him the same <\s>
<s> went up to york to gett a doctor and some hands <\s>
<s> one promist him to give an answer the next day <\s>
<s> att 10 a hand came on board to list but went away without signing <\s>
<s> he promist to return again his name was john webb <\s>
<s> _tuesday 7th this morning the capt <\s>
<s> went up to york and at last agreed with a doctor that belong'd to capt <\s>
<s> cunningham 28 com'r of one of the privateer's sloop that came in the day before <\s>
<s> his name is william blake a young gentleman well recomended by the gen'n of york <\s>
<s> returned on board and brought with him a chest of medicines a doctor's box which cost Â £ 20 york cur renc y 29 also 10 pistolls and cutlasses <\s>
<s> footnote 28 george cunningham whose commission was ordered may 8 1741 footnote 29 the currencies of the different colonies were in great confusion on account of the various and extensive issues of paper money which was greatly depreciated in value <\s>
<s> apparently a pound in new york currency was in 1741 worth about 2.25 mexican silver dollars a pound in rhode island currency about 85 of a dollar <\s>

<s> gave the people a pale of punch <\s>
<s> of beef and a bb <\s>
<s> _thursday 9th this morning put our vessell on the carreen scrub her and gave her boot tops 30 att 4 pm <\s>
<s> our pilott came on board <\s>
<s> orderd him to attend on saturday morning for then he intended to sail <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch <\s>
<s> footnote 30 after careening a vessel and scrubbing off the ooze and shells etc it was customary to coat the bottom with a mixture of tallow sulphur etc <\s>
<s> this was called giving her boot-tops _friday 10th att 9 am <\s>
<s> the mas'r went in the pinnace to york to fetch the lieut <\s>
<s> came in 2 sloops edwd <\s>
<s> seymore and john pasco in comp'y with a brigt james walker com'r all from antigua 13 days passage but brings no news <\s>
<s> came on board the mas'r with 4 new hands john webb jerem'h henderson william ramsey and jos <\s>
<s> the negro servant to the lieut <\s>
<s> _saturday 11 about 8 am <\s>
<s> vandam 31 came on board to take his leave of the capt <\s>
<s> he brought with him 2 pistolls and an acct <\s>
<s> of the doctors chest and other things found for him which amounts to Â £ 38.2 1 new york currency 32 which is carry to acct <\s>
<s> att 10 the lieut <\s>
<s> and doctor came on board in the pilott boat with the hands that had left us since we were at york only 3 which viz <\s>
<s> webster price and ferrows <\s>
<s> the tide being spent cou'd not sail but resolv'd to sail the next day <\s>
<s> went a shoar to gett some hands that had promist to come on board when we were ready to sail <\s>
<s> vandam went from the side we gave him three guns and three chears <\s>
<s> gave the people a bowl of punch <\s>
<s> footnote 31 this was probably isaac van dam merchant son of president rip van dam <\s>
<s> henderson above means harriman footnote 32 see the account below and notes 29 and 33 _sunday 12th the lieut <\s>
<s> with severall hands that went ashoar the night before came on board with our pilott <\s>
<s> the tide being almost spent coud not sail <\s>
<s> duncan mckenley a fitt person for that post <\s>
<s> he wetted his commission by giving the people a tub of punch <\s>
<s> opened 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _munday 13th weigh'd from stratton island with 61 hands officers included <\s>
<s> anchord about 2 pm <\s>
<s> freebody by the capt <\s>
<s> sent him a list of our hands and an acct <\s>
<s> of our provisions and charges together with the lieut <\s>
<s> name to gett it registred in the admiralty office att rhode island <\s>
<s> quartered the people to the guns viz <\s>
<s> went up to york with seven hands three of which left viz <\s>
<s> northwood colson and taylor <\s>
<s> a sloop came in from newfoundland brings no news also another sloop from bermudas <\s>
<s> _friday 3d att 5 am <\s>
<s> we perceived the three hands that had left us the day before on board the _humming bird privateer who had been inticed by some of the owners to leave us by making of them drunk <\s>
<s> about 10 we saw their canoe going a shoare with our hands in her also joseph ferrow whom we had brought from rhode island and had since rec'd clothes on board but had entered on board that sloop as boatswain <\s>
<s> as soon as they had done watering and returning aboard we mann'd our pinnace and boarded their canoe and took our three hands out of her also joseph ferrow and brought them aboard <\s>
<s> some time after the _humming bird's canoe coming alonside ferrow jumpt in her and they put off our pinnace being hawld up in the tackles <\s>
<s> we immediately lett her down but severall raw hands jumping in her and unfortunately the plug being out she almost filled with water which caused such confusion that the canoe gott on board before we gott from our side <\s>
<s> our hands went on board to demand him but they gott all their arms and wou'd not suffer us to board them <\s>
<s> when they returned wou'd not suffer them to return with their arms to take them out for fear of some accident <\s>
<s> of the little privateer came on board of us to know the reason of the disturbance between his people and ours <\s>
<s> told him the reason and forbid him to carry that fellow away for if he did he might chance to hear of him in the west indies and if he did hee'd go 100 leagues to meet him and hee'd take ten for one and murroone 23 his voyage and send him home to his owners and give his people a good dressing i dont doubt but he'll be as good as his word opened a bb <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning with a great deal of rain <\s>
<s> footnote 23 maroon _saturday 4th this morning about 5 am <\s>
<s> came in a ship from marble head 24 who was bound to so <\s>
<s> she had lost her main mast mizen mast and fore top mast <\s>
<s> in the latitude 35Â ° she mett with a hard gale of wind which caused this dissaster so was obliged to put back and came to new york to refitt <\s>
<s> about 11 clock the _humming bird weighd anchor for philadelphia to gett hands <\s>
<s> with 2 sergeants belonging to capt <\s>
<s> riggs comp 25 came on board to look for some soldiers that was suspected to be on board the _humming bird but the wind and tide proving contrary was obliged to return she laying att coney island <\s>
<s> att 6 came in a ship from lisbon had 7 weeks passage and a sloop from turks island both loaded with salt <\s>
<s> the ship appearing to be a lofty vessell put our people in a panetick fear taking her for a 70 gun ship and as we had severall deserters from the men a war they desired the capt <\s>
<s> to hoist a v reef in the jack and lower our penant for a signal for our pinnace that was then a shoare that if she proved to be a man of war they might gett ashoar and gett clear from the press 26 but it proved quit the contrary for the ship and sloops crew taking us by the signal that we had made for our pinnace for a tender of a man of war that was laying there to press hands they quited their vessells and run a shoare as soon as they saw our pinnace mann'd and made for the bushes <\s>
<s> att night the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch to recover them of their fright <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning all this day <\s>

<s> told him the reason and forbid him to carry that fellow away for if he did he might chance to hear of him in the west indies and if he did hee'd go 100 leagues to meet him and hee'd take ten for one and murroone 23 his voyage and send him home to his owners and give his people a good dressing i dont doubt but he'll be as good as his word opened a bb <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning with a great deal of rain <\s>
<s> footnote 23 maroon _saturday 4th this morning about 5 am <\s>
<s> came in a ship from marble head 24 who was bound to so <\s>
<s> she had lost her main mast mizen mast and fore top mast <\s>
<s> in the latitude 35Â ° she mett with a hard gale of wind which caused this dissaster so was obliged to put back and came to new york to refitt <\s>
<s> about 11 clock the _humming bird weighd anchor for philadelphia to gett hands <\s>
<s> with 2 sergeants belonging to capt <\s>
<s> riggs comp 25 came on board to look for some soldiers that was suspected to be on board the _humming bird but the wind and tide proving contrary was obliged to return she laying att coney island <\s>
<s> att 6 came in a ship from lisbon had 7 weeks passage and a sloop from turks island both loaded with salt <\s>
<s> the ship appearing to be a lofty vessell put our people in a panetick fear taking her for a 70 gun ship and as we had severall deserters from the men a war they desired the capt <\s>
<s> to hoist a v reef in the jack and lower our penant for a signal for our pinnace that was then a shoare that if she proved to be a man of war they might gett ashoar and gett clear from the press 26 but it proved quit the contrary for the ship and sloops crew taking us by the signal that we had made for our pinnace for a tender of a man of war that was laying there to press hands they quited their vessells and run a shoare as soon as they saw our pinnace mann'd and made for the bushes <\s>
<s> att night the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch to recover them of their fright <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning all this day <\s>
<s> footnote 24 marblehead mass footnote 25 richard riggs brother-in-law of john watts was captain of one of the two independent companies of fusiliers stationed at new york footnote 26 press-gang _sunday 5th att 5 am <\s>
<s> shipt a hand mathias sallam <\s>
<s> our mate went a shoar to fill water <\s>
<s> he came on board about 8 and informed us that the two country sloops lay att the hook and only waited for a pilott to bring them up which hope will prove true being all tyred of staying here <\s>
<s> weighd anchor and gott nearer in shoar to gett out of the current <\s>
<s> rainy squally windy weather <\s>
<s> here lyes a brigt <\s>
<s> bound to newfoundland a ship to jamaica and a sloop which att 6 pm <\s>
<s> weigh'd anchor bound to barbadoes loaded with lumber and horses <\s>
<s> of beef and 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> this day being a month since we left our commission port have sett down what quantity of provisions expended with the provisions att broch 27 viz <\s>
<s> of beef 1 bb <\s>
<s> of pork 14 bb <\s>
<s> remains 49-1 2 bb <\s>
<s> of beef 29 bb <\s>
<s> of pork 40 c <\s>
<s> footnote 27 at broach means that had been opened _munday 6th about 6 am <\s>
<s> came in the two country sloops so long waited for <\s>
<s> they had been fitted out to cruise after a spanish privateer that was cruising on the coast and had taken severall of our english vessells also a ship from newfoundland and the _huming bird privateer who had been to meet them to gett some hands <\s>
<s> langoe comm'r of one of the above sloops when he came a longside of us he gave us three chears and we returned him the same <\s>
<s> went up to york to gett a doctor and some hands <\s>
<s> one promist him to give an answer the next day <\s>
<s> att 10 a hand came on board to list but went away without signing <\s>
<s> he promist to return again his name was john webb <\s>
<s> _tuesday 7th this morning the capt <\s>
<s> went up to york and at last agreed with a doctor that belong'd to capt <\s>
<s> cunningham 28 com'r of one of the privateer's sloop that came in the day before <\s>
<s> his name is william blake a young gentleman well recomended by the gen'n of york <\s>
<s> returned on board and brought with him a chest of medicines a doctor's box which cost Â £ 20 york cur renc y 29 also 10 pistolls and cutlasses <\s>
<s> footnote 28 george cunningham whose commission was ordered may 8 1741 footnote 29 the currencies of the different colonies were in great confusion on account of the various and extensive issues of paper money which was greatly depreciated in value <\s>
<s> apparently a pound in new york currency was in 1741 worth about 2.25 mexican silver dollars a pound in rhode island currency about 85 of a dollar <\s>

<s> orderd him to attend on saturday morning for then he intended to sail <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch <\s>
<s> footnote 30 after careening a vessel and scrubbing off the ooze and shells etc it was customary to coat the bottom with a mixture of tallow sulphur etc <\s>
<s> this was called giving her boot-tops _friday 10th att 9 am <\s>
<s> the mas'r went in the pinnace to york to fetch the lieut <\s>
<s> came in 2 sloops edwd <\s>
<s> seymore and john pasco in comp'y with a brigt james walker com'r all from antigua 13 days passage but brings no news <\s>
<s> came on board the mas'r with 4 new hands john webb jerem'h henderson william ramsey and jos <\s>
<s> the negro servant to the lieut <\s>
<s> _saturday 11 about 8 am <\s>
<s> vandam 31 came on board to take his leave of the capt <\s>
<s> he brought with him 2 pistolls and an acct <\s>
<s> of the doctors chest and other things found for him which amounts to Â £ 38.2 1 new york currency 32 which is carry to acct <\s>
<s> att 10 the lieut <\s>
<s> and doctor came on board in the pilott boat with the hands that had left us since we were at york only 3 which viz <\s>
<s> webster price and ferrows <\s>
<s> the tide being spent cou'd not sail but resolv'd to sail the next day <\s>
<s> went a shoar to gett some hands that had promist to come on board when we were ready to sail <\s>
<s> vandam went from the side we gave him three guns and three chears <\s>
<s> gave the people a bowl of punch <\s>
<s> footnote 31 this was probably isaac van dam merchant son of president rip van dam <\s>
<s> henderson above means harriman footnote 32 see the account below and notes 29 and 33 _sunday 12th the lieut <\s>
<s> with severall hands that went ashoar the night before came on board with our pilott <\s>
<s> the tide being almost spent coud not sail <\s>
<s> duncan mckenley a fitt person for that post <\s>
<s> he wetted his commission by giving the people a tub of punch <\s>
<s> opened 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _munday 13th weigh'd from stratton island with 61 hands officers included <\s>
<s> anchord about 2 pm <\s>
<s> freebody by the capt <\s>
<s> sent him a list of our hands and an acct <\s>
<s> of our provisions and charges together with the lieut <\s>
<s> name to gett it registred in the admiralty office att rhode island <\s>
<s> quartered the people to the guns viz <\s>
<s> went up to york with seven hands three of which left viz <\s>
<s> northwood colson and taylor <\s>
<s> a sloop came in from newfoundland brings no news also another sloop from bermudas <\s>
<s> _friday 3d att 5 am <\s>
<s> we perceived the three hands that had left us the day before on board the _humming bird privateer who had been inticed by some of the owners to leave us by making of them drunk <\s>
<s> about 10 we saw their canoe going a shoare with our hands in her also joseph ferrow whom we had brought from rhode island and had since rec'd clothes on board but had entered on board that sloop as boatswain <\s>
<s> as soon as they had done watering and returning aboard we mann'd our pinnace and boarded their canoe and took our three hands out of her also joseph ferrow and brought them aboard <\s>
<s> some time after the _humming bird's canoe coming alonside ferrow jumpt in her and they put off our pinnace being hawld up in the tackles <\s>
<s> we immediately lett her down but severall raw hands jumping in her and unfortunately the plug being out she almost filled with water which caused such confusion that the canoe gott on board before we gott from our side <\s>
<s> our hands went on board to demand him but they gott all their arms and wou'd not suffer us to board them <\s>
<s> when they returned wou'd not suffer them to return with their arms to take them out for fear of some accident <\s>
<s> of the little privateer came on board of us to know the reason of the disturbance between his people and ours <\s>
<s> told him the reason and forbid him to carry that fellow away for if he did he might chance to hear of him in the west indies and if he did hee'd go 100 leagues to meet him and hee'd take ten for one and murroone 23 his voyage and send him home to his owners and give his people a good dressing i dont doubt but he'll be as good as his word opened a bb <\s>

<s> freebody by the capt <\s>
<s> sent him a list of our hands and an acct <\s>
<s> of our provisions and charges together with the lieut <\s>
<s> name to gett it registred in the admiralty office att rhode island <\s>
<s> quartered the people to the guns viz <\s>
<s> went up to york with seven hands three of which left viz <\s>
<s> northwood colson and taylor <\s>
<s> a sloop came in from newfoundland brings no news also another sloop from bermudas <\s>
<s> _friday 3d att 5 am <\s>
<s> we perceived the three hands that had left us the day before on board the _humming bird privateer who had been inticed by some of the owners to leave us by making of them drunk <\s>
<s> about 10 we saw their canoe going a shoare with our hands in her also joseph ferrow whom we had brought from rhode island and had since rec'd clothes on board but had entered on board that sloop as boatswain <\s>
<s> as soon as they had done watering and returning aboard we mann'd our pinnace and boarded their canoe and took our three hands out of her also joseph ferrow and brought them aboard <\s>
<s> some time after the _humming bird's canoe coming alonside ferrow jumpt in her and they put off our pinnace being hawld up in the tackles <\s>
<s> we immediately lett her down but severall raw hands jumping in her and unfortunately the plug being out she almost filled with water which caused such confusion that the canoe gott on board before we gott from our side <\s>
<s> our hands went on board to demand him but they gott all their arms and wou'd not suffer us to board them <\s>
<s> when they returned wou'd not suffer them to return with their arms to take them out for fear of some accident <\s>
<s> of the little privateer came on board of us to know the reason of the disturbance between his people and ours <\s>
<s> told him the reason and forbid him to carry that fellow away for if he did he might chance to hear of him in the west indies and if he did hee'd go 100 leagues to meet him and hee'd take ten for one and murroone 23 his voyage and send him home to his owners and give his people a good dressing i dont doubt but he'll be as good as his word opened a bb <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning with a great deal of rain <\s>
<s> footnote 23 maroon _saturday 4th this morning about 5 am <\s>
<s> came in a ship from marble head 24 who was bound to so <\s>
<s> she had lost her main mast mizen mast and fore top mast <\s>
<s> in the latitude 35Â ° she mett with a hard gale of wind which caused this dissaster so was obliged to put back and came to new york to refitt <\s>
<s> about 11 clock the _humming bird weighd anchor for philadelphia to gett hands <\s>
<s> with 2 sergeants belonging to capt <\s>
<s> riggs comp 25 came on board to look for some soldiers that was suspected to be on board the _humming bird but the wind and tide proving contrary was obliged to return she laying att coney island <\s>
<s> att 6 came in a ship from lisbon had 7 weeks passage and a sloop from turks island both loaded with salt <\s>
<s> the ship appearing to be a lofty vessell put our people in a panetick fear taking her for a 70 gun ship and as we had severall deserters from the men a war they desired the capt <\s>
<s> to hoist a v reef in the jack and lower our penant for a signal for our pinnace that was then a shoare that if she proved to be a man of war they might gett ashoar and gett clear from the press 26 but it proved quit the contrary for the ship and sloops crew taking us by the signal that we had made for our pinnace for a tender of a man of war that was laying there to press hands they quited their vessells and run a shoare as soon as they saw our pinnace mann'd and made for the bushes <\s>
<s> att night the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch to recover them of their fright <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning all this day <\s>
<s> footnote 24 marblehead mass footnote 25 richard riggs brother-in-law of john watts was captain of one of the two independent companies of fusiliers stationed at new york footnote 26 press-gang _sunday 5th att 5 am <\s>
<s> shipt a hand mathias sallam <\s>
<s> our mate went a shoar to fill water <\s>
<s> he came on board about 8 and informed us that the two country sloops lay att the hook and only waited for a pilott to bring them up which hope will prove true being all tyred of staying here <\s>
<s> weighd anchor and gott nearer in shoar to gett out of the current <\s>
<s> rainy squally windy weather <\s>
<s> here lyes a brigt <\s>
<s> bound to newfoundland a ship to jamaica and a sloop which att 6 pm <\s>
<s> weigh'd anchor bound to barbadoes loaded with lumber and horses <\s>
<s> of beef and 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> this day being a month since we left our commission port have sett down what quantity of provisions expended with the provisions att broch 27 viz <\s>
<s> of beef 1 bb <\s>
<s> of pork 14 bb <\s>
<s> remains 49-1 2 bb <\s>
<s> of beef 29 bb <\s>
<s> of pork 40 c <\s>
<s> footnote 27 at broach means that had been opened _munday 6th about 6 am <\s>
<s> came in the two country sloops so long waited for <\s>
<s> they had been fitted out to cruise after a spanish privateer that was cruising on the coast and had taken severall of our english vessells also a ship from newfoundland and the _huming bird privateer who had been to meet them to gett some hands <\s>
<s> langoe comm'r of one of the above sloops when he came a longside of us he gave us three chears and we returned him the same <\s>
<s> went up to york to gett a doctor and some hands <\s>
<s> one promist him to give an answer the next day <\s>
<s> att 10 a hand came on board to list but went away without signing <\s>
<s> he promist to return again his name was john webb <\s>
<s> _tuesday 7th this morning the capt <\s>
<s> went up to york and at last agreed with a doctor that belong'd to capt <\s>
<s> cunningham 28 com'r of one of the privateer's sloop that came in the day before <\s>
<s> his name is william blake a young gentleman well recomended by the gen'n of york <\s>
<s> returned on board and brought with him a chest of medicines a doctor's box which cost Â £ 20 york cur renc y 29 also 10 pistolls and cutlasses <\s>
<s> footnote 28 george cunningham whose commission was ordered may 8 1741 footnote 29 the currencies of the different colonies were in great confusion on account of the various and extensive issues of paper money which was greatly depreciated in value <\s>
<s> apparently a pound in new york currency was in 1741 worth about 2.25 mexican silver dollars a pound in rhode island currency about 85 of a dollar <\s>
<s> douglass _summary_ boston 1749 1750 i <\s>

<s> the mate went a shoar to fill water and the mas'r when the mate returned went to gett wood <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch <\s>
<s> of beef and a bb <\s>
<s> _thursday 9th this morning put our vessell on the carreen scrub her and gave her boot tops 30 att 4 pm <\s>
<s> our pilott came on board <\s>
<s> orderd him to attend on saturday morning for then he intended to sail <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch <\s>
<s> footnote 30 after careening a vessel and scrubbing off the ooze and shells etc it was customary to coat the bottom with a mixture of tallow sulphur etc <\s>
<s> this was called giving her boot-tops _friday 10th att 9 am <\s>
<s> the mas'r went in the pinnace to york to fetch the lieut <\s>
<s> came in 2 sloops edwd <\s>
<s> seymore and john pasco in comp'y with a brigt james walker com'r all from antigua 13 days passage but brings no news <\s>
<s> came on board the mas'r with 4 new hands john webb jerem'h henderson william ramsey and jos <\s>
<s> the negro servant to the lieut <\s>
<s> _saturday 11 about 8 am <\s>
<s> vandam 31 came on board to take his leave of the capt <\s>
<s> he brought with him 2 pistolls and an acct <\s>
<s> of the doctors chest and other things found for him which amounts to Â £ 38.2 1 new york currency 32 which is carry to acct <\s>
<s> att 10 the lieut <\s>
<s> and doctor came on board in the pilott boat with the hands that had left us since we were at york only 3 which viz <\s>
<s> webster price and ferrows <\s>
<s> the tide being spent cou'd not sail but resolv'd to sail the next day <\s>
<s> went a shoar to gett some hands that had promist to come on board when we were ready to sail <\s>
<s> vandam went from the side we gave him three guns and three chears <\s>
<s> gave the people a bowl of punch <\s>

<s> came on board the mas'r with 4 new hands john webb jerem'h henderson william ramsey and jos <\s>
<s> the negro servant to the lieut <\s>
<s> _saturday 11 about 8 am <\s>
<s> vandam 31 came on board to take his leave of the capt <\s>
<s> he brought with him 2 pistolls and an acct <\s>
<s> of the doctors chest and other things found for him which amounts to Â £ 38.2 1 new york currency 32 which is carry to acct <\s>
<s> att 10 the lieut <\s>
<s> and doctor came on board in the pilott boat with the hands that had left us since we were at york only 3 which viz <\s>
<s> webster price and ferrows <\s>
<s> the tide being spent cou'd not sail but resolv'd to sail the next day <\s>
<s> went a shoar to gett some hands that had promist to come on board when we were ready to sail <\s>
<s> vandam went from the side we gave him three guns and three chears <\s>
<s> gave the people a bowl of punch <\s>
<s> footnote 31 this was probably isaac van dam merchant son of president rip van dam <\s>
<s> henderson above means harriman footnote 32 see the account below and notes 29 and 33 _sunday 12th the lieut <\s>
<s> with severall hands that went ashoar the night before came on board with our pilott <\s>
<s> the tide being almost spent coud not sail <\s>
<s> duncan mckenley a fitt person for that post <\s>
<s> he wetted his commission by giving the people a tub of punch <\s>
<s> opened 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _munday 13th weigh'd from stratton island with 61 hands officers included <\s>
<s> anchord about 2 pm <\s>
<s> freebody by the capt <\s>
<s> sent him a list of our hands and an acct <\s>
<s> of our provisions and charges together with the lieut <\s>
<s> name to gett it registred in the admiralty office att rhode island <\s>
<s> quartered the people to the guns viz <\s>
<s> went up to york with seven hands three of which left viz <\s>
<s> northwood colson and taylor <\s>
<s> a sloop came in from newfoundland brings no news also another sloop from bermudas <\s>
<s> _friday 3d att 5 am <\s>
<s> we perceived the three hands that had left us the day before on board the _humming bird privateer who had been inticed by some of the owners to leave us by making of them drunk <\s>
<s> about 10 we saw their canoe going a shoare with our hands in her also joseph ferrow whom we had brought from rhode island and had since rec'd clothes on board but had entered on board that sloop as boatswain <\s>
<s> as soon as they had done watering and returning aboard we mann'd our pinnace and boarded their canoe and took our three hands out of her also joseph ferrow and brought them aboard <\s>
<s> some time after the _humming bird's canoe coming alonside ferrow jumpt in her and they put off our pinnace being hawld up in the tackles <\s>
<s> we immediately lett her down but severall raw hands jumping in her and unfortunately the plug being out she almost filled with water which caused such confusion that the canoe gott on board before we gott from our side <\s>
<s> our hands went on board to demand him but they gott all their arms and wou'd not suffer us to board them <\s>
<s> when they returned wou'd not suffer them to return with their arms to take them out for fear of some accident <\s>
<s> of the little privateer came on board of us to know the reason of the disturbance between his people and ours <\s>
<s> told him the reason and forbid him to carry that fellow away for if he did he might chance to hear of him in the west indies and if he did hee'd go 100 leagues to meet him and hee'd take ten for one and murroone 23 his voyage and send him home to his owners and give his people a good dressing i dont doubt but he'll be as good as his word opened a bb <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning with a great deal of rain <\s>
<s> footnote 23 maroon _saturday 4th this morning about 5 am <\s>
<s> came in a ship from marble head 24 who was bound to so <\s>
<s> she had lost her main mast mizen mast and fore top mast <\s>
<s> in the latitude 35Â ° she mett with a hard gale of wind which caused this dissaster so was obliged to put back and came to new york to refitt <\s>
<s> about 11 clock the _humming bird weighd anchor for philadelphia to gett hands <\s>
<s> with 2 sergeants belonging to capt <\s>
<s> riggs comp 25 came on board to look for some soldiers that was suspected to be on board the _humming bird but the wind and tide proving contrary was obliged to return she laying att coney island <\s>
<s> att 6 came in a ship from lisbon had 7 weeks passage and a sloop from turks island both loaded with salt <\s>
<s> the ship appearing to be a lofty vessell put our people in a panetick fear taking her for a 70 gun ship and as we had severall deserters from the men a war they desired the capt <\s>
<s> to hoist a v reef in the jack and lower our penant for a signal for our pinnace that was then a shoare that if she proved to be a man of war they might gett ashoar and gett clear from the press 26 but it proved quit the contrary for the ship and sloops crew taking us by the signal that we had made for our pinnace for a tender of a man of war that was laying there to press hands they quited their vessells and run a shoare as soon as they saw our pinnace mann'd and made for the bushes <\s>
<s> att night the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch to recover them of their fright <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning all this day <\s>
<s> footnote 24 marblehead mass footnote 25 richard riggs brother-in-law of john watts was captain of one of the two independent companies of fusiliers stationed at new york footnote 26 press-gang _sunday 5th att 5 am <\s>
<s> shipt a hand mathias sallam <\s>
<s> our mate went a shoar to fill water <\s>
<s> he came on board about 8 and informed us that the two country sloops lay att the hook and only waited for a pilott to bring them up which hope will prove true being all tyred of staying here <\s>
<s> weighd anchor and gott nearer in shoar to gett out of the current <\s>
<s> rainy squally windy weather <\s>
<s> here lyes a brigt <\s>
<s> bound to newfoundland a ship to jamaica and a sloop which att 6 pm <\s>
<s> weigh'd anchor bound to barbadoes loaded with lumber and horses <\s>
<s> of beef and 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> this day being a month since we left our commission port have sett down what quantity of provisions expended with the provisions att broch 27 viz <\s>
<s> of beef 1 bb <\s>
<s> of pork 14 bb <\s>
<s> remains 49-1 2 bb <\s>
<s> of beef 29 bb <\s>
<s> of pork 40 c <\s>
<s> footnote 27 at broach means that had been opened _munday 6th about 6 am <\s>
<s> came in the two country sloops so long waited for <\s>
<s> they had been fitted out to cruise after a spanish privateer that was cruising on the coast and had taken severall of our english vessells also a ship from newfoundland and the _huming bird privateer who had been to meet them to gett some hands <\s>
<s> langoe comm'r of one of the above sloops when he came a longside of us he gave us three chears and we returned him the same <\s>
<s> went up to york to gett a doctor and some hands <\s>
<s> one promist him to give an answer the next day <\s>
<s> att 10 a hand came on board to list but went away without signing <\s>
<s> he promist to return again his name was john webb <\s>
<s> _tuesday 7th this morning the capt <\s>
<s> went up to york and at last agreed with a doctor that belong'd to capt <\s>
<s> cunningham 28 com'r of one of the privateer's sloop that came in the day before <\s>
<s> his name is william blake a young gentleman well recomended by the gen'n of york <\s>
<s> returned on board and brought with him a chest of medicines a doctor's box which cost Â £ 20 york cur renc y 29 also 10 pistolls and cutlasses <\s>
<s> footnote 28 george cunningham whose commission was ordered may 8 1741 footnote 29 the currencies of the different colonies were in great confusion on account of the various and extensive issues of paper money which was greatly depreciated in value <\s>
<s> apparently a pound in new york currency was in 1741 worth about 2.25 mexican silver dollars a pound in rhode island currency about 85 of a dollar <\s>

<s> his name is william blake a young gentleman well recomended by the gen'n of york <\s>
<s> returned on board and brought with him a chest of medicines a doctor's box which cost Â £ 20 york cur renc y 29 also 10 pistolls and cutlasses <\s>

<s> footnote 30 after careening a vessel and scrubbing off the ooze and shells etc it was customary to coat the bottom with a mixture of tallow sulphur etc <\s>
<s> this was called giving her boot-tops _friday 10th att 9 am <\s>
<s> the mas'r went in the pinnace to york to fetch the lieut <\s>
<s> came in 2 sloops edwd <\s>
<s> seymore and john pasco in comp'y with a brigt james walker com'r all from antigua 13 days passage but brings no news <\s>
<s> came on board the mas'r with 4 new hands john webb jerem'h henderson william ramsey and jos <\s>
<s> the negro servant to the lieut <\s>
<s> _saturday 11 about 8 am <\s>
<s> vandam 31 came on board to take his leave of the capt <\s>
<s> he brought with him 2 pistolls and an acct <\s>
<s> of the doctors chest and other things found for him which amounts to Â £ 38.2 1 new york currency 32 which is carry to acct <\s>
<s> att 10 the lieut <\s>
<s> and doctor came on board in the pilott boat with the hands that had left us since we were at york only 3 which viz <\s>
<s> webster price and ferrows <\s>
<s> the tide being spent cou'd not sail but resolv'd to sail the next day <\s>
<s> went a shoar to gett some hands that had promist to come on board when we were ready to sail <\s>
<s> vandam went from the side we gave him three guns and three chears <\s>
<s> gave the people a bowl of punch <\s>
<s> footnote 31 this was probably isaac van dam merchant son of president rip van dam <\s>
<s> henderson above means harriman footnote 32 see the account below and notes 29 and 33 _sunday 12th the lieut <\s>
<s> with severall hands that went ashoar the night before came on board with our pilott <\s>
<s> the tide being almost spent coud not sail <\s>
<s> duncan mckenley a fitt person for that post <\s>
<s> he wetted his commission by giving the people a tub of punch <\s>
<s> opened 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _munday 13th weigh'd from stratton island with 61 hands officers included <\s>
<s> anchord about 2 pm <\s>
<s> freebody by the capt <\s>
<s> sent him a list of our hands and an acct <\s>
<s> of our provisions and charges together with the lieut <\s>
<s> name to gett it registred in the admiralty office att rhode island <\s>
<s> quartered the people to the guns viz <\s>
<s> went up to york with seven hands three of which left viz <\s>
<s> northwood colson and taylor <\s>
<s> a sloop came in from newfoundland brings no news also another sloop from bermudas <\s>
<s> _friday 3d att 5 am <\s>
<s> we perceived the three hands that had left us the day before on board the _humming bird privateer who had been inticed by some of the owners to leave us by making of them drunk <\s>
<s> about 10 we saw their canoe going a shoare with our hands in her also joseph ferrow whom we had brought from rhode island and had since rec'd clothes on board but had entered on board that sloop as boatswain <\s>
<s> as soon as they had done watering and returning aboard we mann'd our pinnace and boarded their canoe and took our three hands out of her also joseph ferrow and brought them aboard <\s>
<s> some time after the _humming bird's canoe coming alonside ferrow jumpt in her and they put off our pinnace being hawld up in the tackles <\s>
<s> we immediately lett her down but severall raw hands jumping in her and unfortunately the plug being out she almost filled with water which caused such confusion that the canoe gott on board before we gott from our side <\s>
<s> our hands went on board to demand him but they gott all their arms and wou'd not suffer us to board them <\s>
<s> when they returned wou'd not suffer them to return with their arms to take them out for fear of some accident <\s>
<s> of the little privateer came on board of us to know the reason of the disturbance between his people and ours <\s>
<s> told him the reason and forbid him to carry that fellow away for if he did he might chance to hear of him in the west indies and if he did hee'd go 100 leagues to meet him and hee'd take ten for one and murroone 23 his voyage and send him home to his owners and give his people a good dressing i dont doubt but he'll be as good as his word opened a bb <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning with a great deal of rain <\s>
<s> footnote 23 maroon _saturday 4th this morning about 5 am <\s>
<s> came in a ship from marble head 24 who was bound to so <\s>
<s> she had lost her main mast mizen mast and fore top mast <\s>
<s> in the latitude 35Â ° she mett with a hard gale of wind which caused this dissaster so was obliged to put back and came to new york to refitt <\s>
<s> about 11 clock the _humming bird weighd anchor for philadelphia to gett hands <\s>
<s> with 2 sergeants belonging to capt <\s>
<s> riggs comp 25 came on board to look for some soldiers that was suspected to be on board the _humming bird but the wind and tide proving contrary was obliged to return she laying att coney island <\s>
<s> att 6 came in a ship from lisbon had 7 weeks passage and a sloop from turks island both loaded with salt <\s>
<s> the ship appearing to be a lofty vessell put our people in a panetick fear taking her for a 70 gun ship and as we had severall deserters from the men a war they desired the capt <\s>
<s> to hoist a v reef in the jack and lower our penant for a signal for our pinnace that was then a shoare that if she proved to be a man of war they might gett ashoar and gett clear from the press 26 but it proved quit the contrary for the ship and sloops crew taking us by the signal that we had made for our pinnace for a tender of a man of war that was laying there to press hands they quited their vessells and run a shoare as soon as they saw our pinnace mann'd and made for the bushes <\s>
<s> att night the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch to recover them of their fright <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning all this day <\s>
<s> footnote 24 marblehead mass footnote 25 richard riggs brother-in-law of john watts was captain of one of the two independent companies of fusiliers stationed at new york footnote 26 press-gang _sunday 5th att 5 am <\s>
<s> shipt a hand mathias sallam <\s>
<s> our mate went a shoar to fill water <\s>
<s> he came on board about 8 and informed us that the two country sloops lay att the hook and only waited for a pilott to bring them up which hope will prove true being all tyred of staying here <\s>
<s> weighd anchor and gott nearer in shoar to gett out of the current <\s>
<s> rainy squally windy weather <\s>
<s> here lyes a brigt <\s>
<s> bound to newfoundland a ship to jamaica and a sloop which att 6 pm <\s>
<s> weigh'd anchor bound to barbadoes loaded with lumber and horses <\s>
<s> of beef and 1 tierce of bread <\s>

<s> of beef 29 bb <\s>

<s> came in the two country sloops so long waited for <\s>
<s> they had been fitted out to cruise after a spanish privateer that was cruising on the coast and had taken severall of our english vessells also a ship from newfoundland and the _huming bird privateer who had been to meet them to gett some hands <\s>

<s> with severall hands that went ashoar the night before came on board with our pilott <\s>
<s> the tide being almost spent coud not sail <\s>
<s> duncan mckenley a fitt person for that post <\s>
<s> he wetted his commission by giving the people a tub of punch <\s>
<s> opened 1 tierce of bread <\s>
<s> _munday 13th weigh'd from stratton island with 61 hands officers included <\s>
<s> anchord about 2 pm <\s>
<s> freebody by the capt <\s>
<s> sent him a list of our hands and an acct <\s>
<s> of our provisions and charges together with the lieut <\s>
<s> name to gett it registred in the admiralty office att rhode island <\s>
<s> quartered the people to the guns viz <\s>
<s> went up to york with seven hands three of which left viz <\s>
<s> northwood colson and taylor <\s>
<s> a sloop came in from newfoundland brings no news also another sloop from bermudas <\s>
<s> _friday 3d att 5 am <\s>
<s> we perceived the three hands that had left us the day before on board the _humming bird privateer who had been inticed by some of the owners to leave us by making of them drunk <\s>
<s> about 10 we saw their canoe going a shoare with our hands in her also joseph ferrow whom we had brought from rhode island and had since rec'd clothes on board but had entered on board that sloop as boatswain <\s>
<s> as soon as they had done watering and returning aboard we mann'd our pinnace and boarded their canoe and took our three hands out of her also joseph ferrow and brought them aboard <\s>
<s> some time after the _humming bird's canoe coming alonside ferrow jumpt in her and they put off our pinnace being hawld up in the tackles <\s>
<s> we immediately lett her down but severall raw hands jumping in her and unfortunately the plug being out she almost filled with water which caused such confusion that the canoe gott on board before we gott from our side <\s>
<s> our hands went on board to demand him but they gott all their arms and wou'd not suffer us to board them <\s>
<s> when they returned wou'd not suffer them to return with their arms to take them out for fear of some accident <\s>
<s> of the little privateer came on board of us to know the reason of the disturbance between his people and ours <\s>
<s> told him the reason and forbid him to carry that fellow away for if he did he might chance to hear of him in the west indies and if he did hee'd go 100 leagues to meet him and hee'd take ten for one and murroone 23 his voyage and send him home to his owners and give his people a good dressing i dont doubt but he'll be as good as his word opened a bb <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning with a great deal of rain <\s>
<s> footnote 23 maroon _saturday 4th this morning about 5 am <\s>
<s> came in a ship from marble head 24 who was bound to so <\s>
<s> she had lost her main mast mizen mast and fore top mast <\s>
<s> in the latitude 35Â ° she mett with a hard gale of wind which caused this dissaster so was obliged to put back and came to new york to refitt <\s>
<s> about 11 clock the _humming bird weighd anchor for philadelphia to gett hands <\s>
<s> with 2 sergeants belonging to capt <\s>
<s> riggs comp 25 came on board to look for some soldiers that was suspected to be on board the _humming bird but the wind and tide proving contrary was obliged to return she laying att coney island <\s>
<s> att 6 came in a ship from lisbon had 7 weeks passage and a sloop from turks island both loaded with salt <\s>
<s> the ship appearing to be a lofty vessell put our people in a panetick fear taking her for a 70 gun ship and as we had severall deserters from the men a war they desired the capt <\s>
<s> to hoist a v reef in the jack and lower our penant for a signal for our pinnace that was then a shoare that if she proved to be a man of war they might gett ashoar and gett clear from the press 26 but it proved quit the contrary for the ship and sloops crew taking us by the signal that we had made for our pinnace for a tender of a man of war that was laying there to press hands they quited their vessells and run a shoare as soon as they saw our pinnace mann'd and made for the bushes <\s>
<s> att night the capt <\s>
<s> gave the people a pale of punch to recover them of their fright <\s>
<s> thunder and lightning all this day <\s>
